| The cache key is the two-element tuple `['messages', scopeKey] as const` where `scopeKey` is `'channel:<id>'`, `'dm:<id>'`, or `null`                                                                                                                   | Separate key families (`['channel-messages', id]` vs `['dm-messages', id]`); a three-element `['messages', type, id]` | One key family with a discriminator-prefixed scope keeps every cache entry unique while letting the socket handler perform a single `setQueryData` lookup; `as const` satisfies the typed `TQueryKey` generic. The fetch is gated `enabled: token !== null && scopeKey !== null`, so a logged-out caller or an unscoped mount never fires a request                                                                     | Slightly less self-describing than split key families in the React Query devtools; a cosmetic trade-off                                                                                                                    |
| Infinite scroll uses a callback `sentinelRef` that (re)installs an `IntersectionObserver` with `rootMargin: '200px 0px 0px 0px'`, calls `void fetchNextPage()` on intersection, and is backstopped by an unmount-cleanup `useEffect`                    | A `useRef` + `useEffect` observer wired to a stored node; a scroll-event listener; `rootMargin: 0`/`500px`            | A callback ref attaches/detaches the observer exactly when React mounts/replaces the sentinel node and behaves correctly under React 19 strict-mode double-mount; the 200 px top margin prefetches the next page just before the sentinel is visible for flicker-free scrolling; `void` discards the returned promise to satisfy `no-floating-promises` (Rule 3)                                                        | A very fast scroll could outrun a single page fetch — bounded because `fetchNextPage` early-returns while `!hasNextPage \|\| isFetchingNextPage`, preventing overlapping fetches                                           |
| `fetchNextPage` is a `useCallback` depending on the whole `[query]` object and early-returns unless `hasNextPage && !isFetchingNextPage`                                                                                                                | Depend on the spread fields `[query.hasNextPage, query.isFetchingNextPage, query.fetchNextPage]`; no `useCallback`    | TanStack returns a stable result identity per render, so the whole-object dependency is lint-clean under `react-hooks/exhaustive-deps` and avoids enumerating volatile fields; the guard prevents sentinel re-intersection from thrashing an in-flight fetch                                                                                                                                                            | `fetchNextPage` is re-created slightly more often than with a hand-picked dep list, with no behavioural impact (the observer simply re-binds the same logic)                                                               |
| DEVIATION from this file's agent-prompt "exact imports": `PAGE_SIZE` and `MessageWithAuthor` are imported from `@app/shared/*`, not the prompt's illustrative `@blitzy-slack/shared/*`                                                                  | Keep the literal `@blitzy-slack/shared` specifiers the agent prompt printed                                           | The workspace package is scoped `@app/shared` (its `package.json` `name`, the web package's `@app/shared` `workspace:*` dependency, and every sibling hook — `useChannels.ts`, `usePresence.ts`, `useSocket.ts` — import from `@app/shared/*`); `@blitzy-slack/shared` resolves to no package and would fail `tsc`/Vite (Rule 3). Mirrors the recorded `@app/*` precedent for `useChannels`, the auth route, and others | None functional — this aligns the import with the real workspace name; a future monorepo rescope must change every `@app/*` specifier together                                                                             |
| DEVIATION from the agent-prompt skeleton: the `queryFn` returns `await apiClient.get(...)` (rather than the skeleton's bare `return apiClient.get(...)` inside an `async` body), and explicit return types are added to the callbacks                   | Drop `async` from `queryFn`; keep the bare `return` and disable the rule (forbidden by Rule 3)                        | An `async` function with no `await` trips `@typescript-eslint/require-await` (enabled via `recommendedTypeChecked`), which fails the zero-warning build; awaiting the single promise satisfies the rule with identical behaviour (`return-await` is not enabled, so it is safe), and explicit callback return types match the file's strict-typing self-check                                                           | Negligible — `await` on the lone returned promise is behaviourally equivalent to returning it; the extra microtask tick is immaterial                                                                                      |

## `packages/web` — Typing-indicator hook (`src/hooks/useTyping.ts`)

Decisions for the typing-indicator orchestration hook that backs the channel and DM message composers (AAP §0.1.1 "every new message, reaction, typing indicator, and presence change is pushed over Socket.io"; §0.4.5 real-time `typing:start` / `typing:stop` contract; §0.8.4 typed Socket.io events). It owns both the outgoing throttle (a `typing:start` at most once per 3 s while typing, an auto `typing:stop` after 5 s of inactivity or on an explicit `stopTyping()`) and the incoming side (a scope-filtered, self-echo-filtered `typingUsers: string[]` with a 5 s per-user expiry safety net), behind the `UseTypingResult` surface consumed by the (planned) `MessageComposer.tsx`.

| What was decided                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | What alternatives existed                                                                                            | Why this choice was made                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | What risks it carries                                                                                                                             |
| --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| DEVIATION from this file's agent-prompt "Phase 1: Imports": `ServerToClientEvents` is imported (type-only) from `@app/shared/types/socket-events`, not the prompt's illustrative `@blitzy-slack/shared/types/socket-events`                                     | Keep the literal `@blitzy-slack/shared` specifier the agent prompt printed                                           | The workspace package is scoped `@app/shared` — confirmed by `packages/shared/package.json` `name`, its `exports` map (`"./types/*": "./src/types/*.ts"`), the web package's `@app/shared` `workspace:*` dependency, and the sibling `useSocket.ts` / `auth.store.ts` both importing `@app/shared/types/*`; `@blitzy-slack/shared` resolves to no package and would fail `tsc` / Vite (Rule 3). Mirrors the `@app/*` precedent already recorded for `useChannels`, `useSocket`, `useMessages`, `@app/db`, and `@app/web`                                                                                             | None functional — this aligns the import with the real workspace name; a future monorepo rescope must change every `@app/*` specifier together    |
| DEVIATION from the agent-prompt's Phase-5 sketch (a bare `const scope = channelId !== undefined ? { channelId } : dmId !== undefined ? { dmId } : null`): `scope` is wrapped in `useMemo(..., [channelId, dmId])`, and `useMemo` is added to the `react` import | Keep the inline ternary the prompt printed; disable `react-hooks/exhaustive-deps` for the file (forbidden by Rule 3) | An inline ternary rebuilds the `scope` object every render, so the `notifyTyping` / `stopTyping` `useCallback`s that close over it would change identity each render — `react-hooks/exhaustive-deps` flags this and demands `useMemo`, failing the zero-warning build. Verified empirically: a throwaway probe restoring the inline ternary emitted exactly two `exhaustive-deps` warnings ("wrap the initialization of 'scope' in its own useMemo() Hook"), and wrapping it in `useMemo([channelId, dmId])` cleared them with no behavioural change (`scope` recomputes only when `channelId` / `dmId` transitions) | None functional — `useMemo` only stabilises the object identity; a future edit changing the `scope` inputs must keep them in the dependency array |
| Outgoing emits are gated by `THROTTLE_INTERVAL_MS = 3_000` (at most one `typing:start` per 3 s of continuous typing) with an auto `typing:stop` after `INACTIVITY_TIMEOUT_MS = 5_000` of no further `notifyTyping()` calls                                      | 1 s / 3 s (snappier, more emits); 5 s / 10 s (fewer emits, laggier); no throttle (one emit per keystroke)            | A ~3 s emission cadence matches Slack's perceived typing-indicator rhythm while bounding network load to one event per 3 s, and a 5 s inactivity window matches a natural typing pause before the indicator clears; emitting per keystroke would flood the server (the explicit anti-pattern in the file spec)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | If the user pauses then resumes within 3 s the indicator stays continuous — the intended behaviour, not a defect                                  |
| Each incoming `typing:start` (re)arms a per-user `REMOTE_EXPIRY_MS = 5_000` timer that removes the user from `typingUsers` even when no `typing:stop` ever arrives                                                                                              | No expiry (trust `typing:stop` alone); a 10 s expiry                                                                 | A dropped `typing:stop` (network blip, frozen tab, abrupt disconnect) would otherwise pin a stale "is typing…" indicator indefinitely; a 5 s safety net mirrors the inactivity cadence so a genuinely-typing remote keeps renewing its timer while a vanished one clears within 5 s                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | A remote user who navigates away mid-typing shows as typing for up to 5 s; acceptable and self-correcting                                         |
| The local user's own `typing:start` echoes are suppressed via `currentUserId !== null && payload.userId === currentUserId`, reading the id through the `useAuthStore((s) => s.user?.id ?? null)` selector                                                       | Include the local user in `typingUsers`; rely on server-side filtering only                                          | Slack never shows "you are typing" to yourself, and the server may broadcast the sender's own event into the room; a client-side identity filter is the simplest correct guard, and the selector form re-renders the hook only on login/logout identity transitions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | None — the only edge is a logged-out (`null`) id, where the guard short-circuits and no suppression is attempted                                  |
| `typingUsers` carries raw `userId` strings, not resolved `displayName`s                                                                                                                                                                                         | Store `displayName`; store `{ userId, displayName }` objects                                                         | `userId` is stable and arrives directly on the typed `typing:start` payload, whereas display-name resolution is a separate concern owned by the channel-members cache at the UI layer; keeping the hook id-only avoids coupling it to a name lookup it has no data for                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | The consuming UI must map `userId` → `displayName` from elsewhere; an accepted layering boundary documented here                                  |
| Remote expiry timers live in a single `useRef<Map<string, ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>>` keyed by `userId`, not an object literal or per-user state                                                                                                           | An object `{ [userId]: timer }`; per-user `useState` entries                                                         | `Map` `get` / `set` / `delete` are O(1) and immune to prototype-key collisions on arbitrary string ids, and a `useRef` holds the handles across renders without triggering re-renders (timer handles are not render state); storing them in `useState` would re-render on every keystroke (an explicit anti-pattern), and `ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>` keeps the handle type cross-runtime safe                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | None — the `Map` is cleared on `typing:stop`, on per-user expiry, and wholesale in the scope-change / unmount cleanup effect                      |
| The three timings are module-level `const`s, not hook parameters or `UseTypingOptions` fields                                                                                                                                                                   | Accept `throttleMs` / `inactivityMs` / `expiryMs` as `UseTypingOptions` fields                                       | A zero-config API keeps every call site identical and the PoC has a single typing cadence; tuning belongs in this decision log, not spread across call sites, so `UseTypingOptions` stays limited to the `channelId` / `dmId` scope the schema mandates                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | If a future surface needs different tuning the constants must be promoted to options; out of PoC scope and a localised change                     |

## `packages/web` — Channels section (`src/components/channels/ChannelList.tsx`)

Decisions for the sidebar "Channels" section — the composing component that orchestrates the `ChannelListItem` rows and the controlled `CreateChannelDialog` modal (AAP §0.1.1 "list channels", §0.6.2 TanStack-cache pattern, §0.6.3 three-column sidebar layout, Rule 1 screenshots 29 & 100). It sources data from the read-only `useChannels()` TanStack Query hook, renders the loading / empty / error / list states, owns the create-dialog open state, and is mounted once by the downstream `Sidebar.tsx` (deeper agent). The light-lavender active-pill and sidebar-foreground tokens it relies on are defined in the _Theme tokens_ section above.

| What was decided                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | What alternatives existed                                                                                                                                                                          | Why this choice was made                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | What risks it carries                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| DEVIATION from this file's agent-prompt Phase-1/Phase-4 imports and schema `internal_imports`/`external_imports`: the `useSocketEvent` (`@/hooks/useSocket`) and `useQueryClient` (`@tanstack/react-query`) imports and the three prescribed `channel:created` / `channel:member_joined` / `channel:member_left` subscriptions were DROPPED entirely (the "degraded mode" the agent prompt's _Final Note on Event Names_ explicitly sanctions) | Keep the three `useSocketEvent` subscriptions verbatim; subscribe to a single generic `channels:invalidate` event; suppress the resulting type error with `@ts-expect-error` (forbidden by Rule 3) | The shared `ServerToClientEvents` interface (`@app/shared/types/socket-events`) declares ZERO channel-lifecycle events — only `MESSAGE_NEW`, `MESSAGE_UPDATED`, `REACTION_ADDED`, `REACTION_REMOVED`, `PRESENCE_UPDATE`, `TYPING_START`, `TYPING_STOP`, `ERROR` — and `useSocketEvent<E extends keyof ServerToClientEvents>` is strictly typed, so subscribing to a non-existent `channel:*` event is a `tsc` error (TS2345) that fails the zero-warning build (Rule 3). With no subscriptions, `useQueryClient` becomes an unused binding that also fails `noUnusedLocals` / `@typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars`. The channels route (`routes/channels.ts`) confirms channel mutations emit NO Socket.io events by design (see its decision row), so this is the intended architecture, not a missing event. Cache freshness instead relies on `CreateChannelDialog`'s own success-path `queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['channels'] })` plus refetch-on-mount | A channel created/joined/left from ANOTHER browser tab or device does not refresh this sidebar in real time until the next `['channels']` refetch (mount / manual). Accepted for the single-workspace PoC and recorded here as the sanctioned degraded mode; a future per-user `channel:*` server event would let the dropped subscriptions be restored |
| DEVIATION from the agent-prompt Phase-8 JSX (`text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wide text-sidebar-foreground/70`): the `Channels` heading is rendered in SENTENCE case via `text-xs font-semibold text-sidebar-foreground/70` (the `uppercase tracking-wide` utilities were removed)                                                                                                                                                    | Keep the prompt's literal `uppercase tracking-wide` classes                                                                                                                                        | `screenshots/Slack web Jul 2024 29.png` and `100.png` render every sidebar section heading ("Channels", "Direct messages", "Apps", "Starred") in sentence case, not uppercase; Rule 1 ranks the authoritative screenshots above an illustrative prompt class string, and the discrepancy was caught and fixed during the Phase-4 in-browser visual comparison                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | None functional — the change is purely typographic and matches the authoritative screenshot; a reader comparing to the prompt's literal classes is reconciled by this row                                                                                                                                                                               |
| A single icon-only "+" `Button variant="ghost" size="icon"` next to the section heading opens the create dialog — the screenshot-29 "+ Add channels" bottom row is NOT rendered                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Render both the heading "+" and a bottom "+ Add channels" row; render only the bottom row                                                                                                          | Modern Slack web exposes the "+" in both places, but a single heading-adjacent trigger keeps the dense sidebar compact and is the cleaner PoC affordance; the `aria-label="Create channel"` names the icon-only control for assistive tech and the `Plus` glyph is `aria-hidden`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Slight divergence from screenshot 29's explicit "+ Add channels" row; intentional and documented                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| The loading state renders a hard-coded 4 `Skeleton` rows                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Parameterize the count via a prop; derive it from the available sidebar height                                                                                                                     | PoC pragmatism — 4 rows approximate the typical pre-scroll channel count in the sidebar and give a useful loading affordance without measuring layout; index-as-key (`key={i}`) is safe for this static, never-reordered list                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Inflexible if the sidebar height changes dramatically; a future responsive variant could parameterize it — a localized change                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| The fetch-error state is inline destructive-colored text (`text-xs text-destructive`) that includes `error.message`, rendered alongside (not replacing) the header and "+" button                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | A shadcn `Alert variant="destructive"`; a toast; hiding the section entirely on error                                                                                                              | `Alert` is a page-level treatment that is visually too heavy for a compact sidebar section; inline text is minimally intrusive, keeps the header and create affordance usable during an error, and surfaces `error.message` for diagnostics                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Less attention-grabbing than an `Alert`; acceptable because the message text still conveys the failure and the section stays operable                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| The section is rendered ALWAYS-EXPANDED — no collapsible chevron / `Collapsible` wrapper                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Wrap the section body in a Radix `Collapsible` with a chevron toggle on the heading                                                                                                                | The folder spec marks collapsibility as optional and explicitly defers it to a deeper agent; keeping the PoC section always-expanded reduces scope and state                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Divergence from Slack's collapsible section UX; documented for a future enhancement                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| The list is NOT wrapped in a shadcn `ScrollArea`; scrolling is delegated to the parent `Sidebar.tsx`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | Wrap the `<ul>` (or the whole section) in `ScrollArea` here                                                                                                                                        | The parent sidebar layout owns the single overall scroll container for the combined Channels + DMs sections; nesting a `ScrollArea` here would create nested/double scrollbars and fight the parent's scroll                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | None — the parent's single scroll container is the correct ownership boundary                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `ChannelListItem` receives an explicitly narrowed `{ id, name, isPrivate }` object literal, not the full `ChannelWithMembers` row from `useChannels()`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Pass `channel={channel}` (the wider `ChannelWithMembers`, which structurally satisfies the narrower prop)                                                                                          | The explicit narrow object documents exactly which fields the row consumes, matches the `ChannelSummary` contract `ChannelListItem` declares, and reduces coupling so a future `ChannelListItem` `React.memo` can compare a minimal shape; `unreadCount` is intentionally omitted because `ChannelWithMembers` does not carry it (unread counts are a deferred feature)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Slightly more verbose than spreading the whole object; net benefit in contract clarity. If unread counts are later added to the list response, this object must be widened                                                                                                                                                                              |
| The root element is a semantic `<section aria-label="Channels">` landmark; the list is a `<ul>` / `<li key={channel.id}>` and the heading is an `<h2>`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | A non-semantic `<div>` root with class-only styling                                                                                                                                                | The labelled `<section>` is an accessibility landmark screen-reader users can navigate to, the `<ul>`/`<li>` announces the channel count, and `<h2>` nests correctly under the page-level `<h1>` in the channel header — all invisible accessibility with zero visual impact (UI3)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | None                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| The loading skeleton container carries `role="status"` + `aria-label="Loading channels"`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Rely on the `Skeleton` primitive's own ARIA; add `aria-busy` instead                                                                                                                               | The shadcn `Skeleton` primitive is a bare styled `<div>` with no built-in role or accessible name (verified in `ui/skeleton.tsx`), so the wrapper must announce the loading state to assistive tech; `role="status"` with a label is the canonical live-region pattern for an indeterminate load                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | None                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `CreateChannelDialog` is ALWAYS mounted at the end of the section, controlled via `open={isCreateDialogOpen}` / `onOpenChange={setIsCreateDialogOpen}`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Conditionally mount the dialog only while `isCreateDialogOpen === true`                                                                                                                            | The dialog is a Radix-portal primitive that renders nothing visible while closed, so always-mounting is the canonical controlled-dialog pattern and avoids mount/unmount churn and focus-restoration glitches on every open                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | None — the closed dialog has negligible overhead and the portal handles the open/closed lifecycle                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |

## `packages/web` — Channel header (`src/components/channels/ChannelHeader.tsx`)

Decisions for the channel-view top bar rendered above the message timeline by `Channel.tsx` (AAP §0.1.1 channel "leave", §0.5.2 component mapping, §0.7.2 out-of-scope feature exclusions, Rule 1 screenshots 29 & 100). It receives the full `ChannelWithMembers` record via props from the parent `Channel` page, renders the `#` / `Lock` name + optional description + member-count chip + overflow `DropdownMenu`, and owns the controlled Leave-confirmation `Dialog`. The `--color-border` and muted-foreground tokens it relies on are defined in the _Theme tokens_ section above.

| What was decided                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | What alternatives existed                                                                                                                                                  | Why this choice was made                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | What risks it carries                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| The member-count is a no-op `Button variant="ghost" size="sm"` chip with NO `onClick` handler, not a `<span>` and not a working member-list popover                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Render a static non-interactive `<span>`; wire a full member-list `Popover`/panel                                                                                          | The folder spec calls for a "small clickable chip"; a `Button` preserves visual symmetry with Slack's clickable member chip and future-proofs for a member-list popover (a deferred feature with no member-data plumbing in this component), while the `aria-label` carries the count for assistive tech                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | A button with no action is a partial affordance for keyboard/AT users; mitigated by the descriptive `aria-label`; recorded as the sanctioned no-op until a member-list panel agent wires it                                                                            |
| NO Huddle, Canvas, Workflow, Bookmark, or "Settings" dropdown item is rendered in the header                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Render them as disabled buttons; include a "Settings" item opening a placeholder                                                                                           | AAP §0.7.2 lists Huddle/Canvas/Workflow/Bookmark as explicitly out of scope and the folder spec marks channel settings as read-only metadata only; rendering disabled or dead controls would imply features that do not exist                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Visual divergence from screenshot 29 (which shows Huddle/Canvas/+bookmark); intentional and documented per the AAP scope boundary                                                                                                                                      |
| Leave confirmation uses a controlled shadcn `Dialog` (Cancel ghost + destructive Leave), not `window.confirm()`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Browser-native `window.confirm()` / `window.alert()`                                                                                                                       | The shadcn `Dialog` matches Slack's centered modal-overlay pattern (AAP §0.6.3), is accessible (focus trap, Escape-to-close, focus restoration) and themeable; native dialogs are unstyled and break the design language                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | None                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| DEVIATION from this file's agent-prompt Phase-1/Phase-4 imports and schema `internal_imports` (`useSocketEvent` from `@/hooks/useSocket`): the prescribed `channel:member_joined` / `channel:member_left` subscriptions and the `useSocketEvent` import were DROPPED entirely (the "skip socket subscriptions entirely and document the gap" fallback the agent prompt explicitly sanctions) | Keep the two `useSocketEvent` subscriptions verbatim; subscribe to a single `channel:updated` event; suppress the type error with `@ts-expect-error` (forbidden by Rule 3) | The shared `ServerToClientEvents` (`@app/shared/types/socket-events`) declares ZERO channel-lifecycle events — only `MESSAGE_NEW`, `MESSAGE_UPDATED`, `REACTION_ADDED`, `REACTION_REMOVED`, `PRESENCE_UPDATE`, `TYPING_START`, `TYPING_STOP`, `ERROR` — and `useSocketEvent<E extends keyof ServerToClientEvents>` is strictly typed, so subscribing to a non-existent `channel:*` event is a `tsc` TS2345 error that fails the zero-warning build (Rule 3). The `channel:join`/`channel:leave` constants are CLIENT→SERVER room-subscription events `(channelId, ack)`, not server broadcasts, so they are unusable with `useSocketEvent`. This is the identical sanctioned degraded mode already recorded for `ChannelList.tsx`. Member-count freshness instead relies on the leave mutation's own `invalidateQueries(['channels'])` plus refetch-on-mount | A join/leave from ANOTHER tab/device does not refresh this header's member count in real time until the next `['channels']` refetch; accepted for the single-workspace PoC; a future per-user `channel:*` server event would let the dropped subscriptions be restored |
| DEVIATION from the agent-prompt Phase-1 import path `@blitzy-slack/shared/types/channel`: `ChannelWithMembers` is imported from `@app/shared/types/channel`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Use the prompt's literal `@blitzy-slack/shared` specifier                                                                                                                  | The shared workspace package is named `@app/shared` (verified in `packages/shared/package.json` and every existing web import — `ChannelListItem.tsx`, `CreateChannelDialog.tsx`, `useSocket.ts`); the `@blitzy-slack/*` scope in the prompt is an illustrative placeholder that does not resolve and would be a `tsc`/Vite module-not-found error. This reconciles the prompt's seed scope with the implemented `@app/*` scope already recorded in the package-manifest decisions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | None functional — the corrected specifier is the only one that resolves; a reader comparing to the prompt's literal scope is reconciled by this row                                                                                                                    |
| On leave-mutation success, navigate to `/app` (after invalidating `['channels']`, toasting, and closing the dialog)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Stay on the now-left channel route (which would 404 / show an empty state)                                                                                                 | The user explicitly left the channel, so remaining on its route would show a broken/empty view; `/app` is the AAP §0.6.3 default authenticated landing route                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | None significant                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| The channel name is rendered as an `<h1>`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | `<h2>`, or a non-heading `<p>`/`<span>`                                                                                                                                    | The channel view (`/app/channels/:channelId`) is the page's primary content, so its name is the page-level heading; `<h1>` is the semantically correct top heading and the sidebar `ChannelList` `<h2>` nests correctly beneath it                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           | None                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| An `sr-only` `<span>` announces "private channel" / "public channel"; the visual `Lock` icon and `#` glyph are `aria-hidden="true"`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Put an `aria-label` on the icon; rely on the icon alone                                                                                                                    | Decoupling the screen-reader announcement from the decorative visual indicator gives AT users an explicit word while keeping the icon/glyph purely visual (UI3 invisible accessibility, zero visual impact)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | None                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| The member count is pluralized in English — `1 member` vs `N members` — via an explicit `=== 1` check                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Always render "members"; use an i18n/ICU plural formatter                                                                                                                  | Correct singular/plural is a small UX polish that reads naturally; the PoC has no i18n framework, so an inline English check is proportionate                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | English-only; if i18n is later added this must move to an ICU plural rule — a localized change                                                                                                                                                                         |
| BOTH the Cancel and Leave buttons are `disabled` while the leave mutation is pending (Leave shows a "Leaving…" label)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Disable only the Leave button                                                                                                                                              | Disabling Cancel too prevents the user from dismissing the dialog mid-request and leaving the UI in an ambiguous state (request in flight, dialog closed); the loading label gives feedback                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Slight friction if the network is slow (the user cannot abort); acceptable for a single fast mutation                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Member-count freshness after leave uses `queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['channels'] })`, not a per-channel query key or an optimistic update                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | A per-channel `['channel', id]` key; an optimistic `memberCount` mutation                                                                                                  | The displayed count derives from the parent page's `useChannels()` cache (key `['channels']`), so invalidating that one key is the simplest correct refresh and matches the established `CreateChannelDialog` / `useChannels` pattern; optimistic updates are unnecessary at PoC scale                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | A one-roundtrip delay between the action and the refreshed count; acceptable for the PoC                                                                                                                                                                               |
| The bottom divider is `border-b border-border` (explicit token class), not a bare `border-b`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | Bare `border-b` (as the agent-prompt Phase-5 JSX literally showed); add a global `* { border-color: var(--color-border) }` base rule to `src/index.css`                    | Tailwind v4 defaults a bare `border`/`border-b` to `currentColor`, and this project's `src/index.css` `@layer base` intentionally has NO global border-color rule, so a bare `border-b` rendered the divider in the near-black foreground (`oklch(0.145 0 0)`) instead of the subtle `--color-border` gray (`oklch(0.922 0 0)`) that AAP §0.5.3 maps "subtle dividers" to and that screenshots 29 & 100 show. Spelling out `border-border` matches the established convention of the analogous `layout/Header.tsx`, `Landing.tsx`, and `SearchResults.tsx` chrome headers; editing the global stylesheet was rejected as out-of-scope and project-wide-risky. Caught and fixed during the Phase-4 in-browser computed-CSS comparison (verified `border-bottom-color: oklch(0.922 0 0)`)                                                                      | None — the explicit token is the correct, convention-aligned value; a reader comparing to the prompt's literal `border-b` is reconciled by this row                                                                                                                    |

## `packages/web` — Workspace nav rail (`src/components/layout/WorkspaceNavRail.tsx`)

Decisions for the far-left vertical icon rail — the first of the three columns in screenshots 29 & 100 (AAP §0.5.4 "Workspace nav rail" gap resolution, §0.7.2 out-of-scope exclusions, Rule 1, Rule 3). It is a leaf layout component: a static workspace logo, `Home`/`Direct messages` icon buttons that route to `/app`, a spacer, and a profile-avatar `DropdownMenu` with a destructive `Log out`. The `--color-sidebar-*` tokens it relies on are defined in the _Theme tokens_ section above; logout is delegated to `useAuth()`.

| What was decided                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | What alternatives existed                                                                                                                                                    | Why this choice was made                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | What risks it carries                                                                                                                                                               |
| ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| The current-user profile `AvatarFallback` shows the first character of `user.email`, uppercased, via a file-local `getInitial` that returns `'?'` when the email is missing or empty                                                                                                                                    | (a) Fetch a display name via `GET /api/auth/me`; (b) hardcode a generic person icon                                                                                          | The `useAuth` store carries only `{ id, email }` — no `displayName`/`avatarUrl` — and profile fetching/editing is out of scope (AAP §0.7.2), so deriving the initial from `email` needs no extra request and the `'?'` guard means the fallback never renders a blank or `undefined` glyph (UI8)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               | Two users whose emails share a first character collide on the same fallback letter; acceptable visual ambiguity for the PoC                                                         |
| The rail OMITS the Activity / notifications (bell) button visible in screenshots 29/100, rendering only the workspace logo, `Home`, `Direct messages`, and the profile/account menu                                                                                                                                     | Render a static, non-functional Activity button to match the screenshot more closely                                                                                         | AAP §0.7.2 excludes push notifications and the activity feed; a dead button implies an out-of-scope feature and is a worse Rule 1 compromise than omitting an unscoped control — the identical rationale already recorded for the `ChannelHeader` Huddle/Canvas/Workflow omission                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | Minor visual divergence from the reference screenshots; intentional and scope-bounded                                                                                               |
| The rail surface uses `bg-sidebar-bg`, its right divider `border-sidebar-border`, and the icon-button hovers `hover:bg-sidebar-hover hover:text-sidebar-hover-foreground` — a deviation from this file's agent-prompt JSX, which showed `bg-sidebar` and `hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground` | Use the prompt's literal `bg-sidebar` / `hover:bg-sidebar-accent`; introduce a new `--color-sidebar` token; reuse `hover:bg-sidebar-accent/50` (the `ChannelListItem` hover) | `src/index.css` defines NO `--color-sidebar` token, so Tailwind v4 emits no `bg-sidebar` utility and the rail would render with no background (a broken view, UI10); the defined surface token is `--color-sidebar-bg` → `bg-sidebar-bg`. `--color-sidebar-accent` is the light-lavender selected-channel pill (per `ChannelListItem`), wrong as a hover on the dark aubergine rail, whereas `--color-sidebar-hover` (lighter aubergine) + `--color-sidebar-hover-foreground` (near-white) are the purpose-built rail-hover tokens and honour the prompt author's stated intent that "hover states match the aubergine palette". Same explicit-defined-token discipline already recorded for `ChannelHeader`'s `border-border` | None functional — these are the only utilities that resolve to the intended colours; a reader comparing to the prompt's literal class names is reconciled by this row               |
| `handleLogout` calls `useAuth().logout()` synchronously (no `await`) then `void navigate('/login', { replace: true })`; the dropdown item's `onSelect` calls `handleLogout()` directly (no `void`); the two `Link`-backed (`asChild`) nav buttons omit `type="button"`, kept only on the real profile `<button>`        | Keep the prompt's `async () => { await logout(); navigate(...) }` with a bare `navigate(...)`; keep `type="button"` on the `asChild` Link buttons                            | `useAuth().logout()` returns `void`, so `await logout()` trips `@typescript-eslint/await-thenable` and fails the zero-warning build (Rule 3); React Router 7's `NavigateFunction` returns `void \| Promise<void>`, so a bare `navigate(...)` trips `@typescript-eslint/no-floating-promises` — the established repo fix is `void navigate(...)` (used by `ChannelListItem`, `CreateChannelDialog`, `ChannelHeader`, `SearchBar`, `StartDmDialog`). A synchronous handler returns no promise, so `no-misused-promises` needs no `void` wrapper; `type="button"` is invalid on the `<a>` that `asChild` renders and is absent from the canonical shadcn `<Button asChild><Link/></Button>` pattern                               | None functional — behaviour (clear auth, drop the socket, redirect to `/login`) is identical and Rule 3 passes; a reader comparing to the prompt's async snippet is reconciled here |

## `packages/api` — Routes barrel (`src/routes/index.ts`)

Decisions for the top-level `/api` router barrel that composes the seven resource sub-routers (`auth`, `channels`, `dms`, `files`, `health`, `messages`, `search`) into the single `router` symbol `app.ts` mounts at `/api` (AAP §0.6.1 Group 4, §0.6.2, Rule 3). The file is a pure composer: it imports each sub-router's named `router` export via `{ router as XRouter }` aliasing and calls `router.use('/<name>', XRouter)` — no route handlers, no middleware, no catch-all.

| What was decided                                                                                                                                    | What alternatives existed                                                               | Why this choice was made                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | What risks it carries                                                                                                  |
| --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| DEVIATION from this file's agent-prompt skeleton JSDoc tag `@blitzy-slack/api`: the file header uses the `@app/api` scope                           | Keep the prompt's literal `@blitzy-slack/api` tag                                       | The API workspace package is named `@app/api` (verified in `packages/api/package.json`) and every existing sibling route file (`auth.ts`, `health.ts`, …) opens with the `@app/api — …` doc tag; the `@blitzy-slack/*` scope in the prompt is an illustrative placeholder. Using `@app/api` keeps the doc header consistent with the real package name and the sibling house style — the identical `@blitzy-slack/*` → `@app/*` reconciliation already recorded for the web package | None functional — a documentation-only tag; a reader comparing to the prompt's literal scope is reconciled by this row |
| Each sub-router exports `const router: Router` (uniform name) and the barrel aliases on import (`import { router as authRouter } from './auth.js'`) | Have each sub-router export a descriptive name (e.g. `authRouter`); use default exports | A uniform `router` export lets every route file read identically and lets the barrel apply one consistent aliasing pattern; named (non-default) exports are required so the barrel can verify each symbol exists at compile time. Confirmed all seven siblings already export `export const router: Router = Router();` with no default exports                                                                                                                                     | None — slight import verbosity, offset by uniformity                                                                   |
